\DoxyCodeLine{127 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{128 \textcolor{comment}{ * Intel SIMD intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{129 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{130 \textcolor{comment}{ * Preprocessor directives below:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{131 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/ include headers for SSE2/AVX2/AVX2+FMA3 intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{132 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/ defines \_ALGLIB\_HAS\_SSE2\_INTRINSICS, \_ALGLIB\_HAS\_AVX2\_INTRINSICS and \_ALGLIB\_HAS\_FMA\_INTRINSICS definitions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{133 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{134 \textcolor{comment}{ * These actions are performed when we have:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{135 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/ x86 architecture definition (AE\_CPU==AE\_INTEL)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{136 \textcolor{comment}{ * -\/ compiler which supports intrinsics}}
\DoxyCodeLine{137 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{138 \textcolor{comment}{ * Presence of \_ALGLIB\_HAS\_???\_INTRINSICS does NOT mean that our CPU}}
\DoxyCodeLine{139 \textcolor{comment}{ * actually supports these intrinsics -\/ such things should be determined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{140 \textcolor{comment}{ * at runtime with ae\_cpuid() call. It means that we are working under}}
\DoxyCodeLine{141 \textcolor{comment}{ * Intel and out compiler can issue SIMD-\/capable code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{142 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{143 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{147 \textcolor{comment}{     * Intel definitions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{148 \textcolor{comment}{     */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{151 \textcolor{comment}{         * MSVC is detected.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{154 \textcolor{comment}{         */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{429 \textcolor{comment}{/************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{430 \textcolor{comment}{dynamic block which may be automatically deallocated during stack unwinding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{431 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{432 \textcolor{comment}{p\_next          next block in the stack unwinding list.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{433 \textcolor{comment}{                NULL means that this block is not in the list}}
\DoxyCodeLine{434 \textcolor{comment}{deallocator     deallocator function which should be used to deallocate block.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{435 \textcolor{comment}{                NULL for "{}special"{} blocks (frame/stack boundaries)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{436 \textcolor{comment}{ptr             pointer which should be passed to the deallocator.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{437 \textcolor{comment}{                may be null (for zero-\/size block), DYN\_BOTTOM or DYN\_FRAME}}
\DoxyCodeLine{438 \textcolor{comment}{                for "{}special"{} blocks (frame/stack boundaries).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{439 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{440 \textcolor{comment}{valgrind\_hint   is a special field which stores a special hint pointer for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{441 \textcolor{comment}{                Valgrind and other similar memory checking tools.  ALGLIB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{442 \textcolor{comment}{                manually aligns pointers obtained via malloc, so ptr usually}}
\DoxyCodeLine{443 \textcolor{comment}{                points to location past the beginning  of  the  actuallly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{444 \textcolor{comment}{                allocated memory. In such cases memory testing tools  may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{445 \textcolor{comment}{                report "{}(possibly) lost"{} memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{446 \textcolor{comment}{                }}
\DoxyCodeLine{447 \textcolor{comment}{                This "{}hint"{} field stores  pointer  actually  returned  by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{448 \textcolor{comment}{                malloc (or NULL, if for some reason  we  do  not  support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{449 \textcolor{comment}{                this feature). This field is used merely as  a  hint  for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{450 \textcolor{comment}{                Valgrind -\/ it should NOT be used for anything else.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{451 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{452 \textcolor{comment}{************************************************************************/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{539 }
\DoxyCodeLine{540 \textcolor{comment}{/************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{541 \textcolor{comment}{Serializer:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{542 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{543 \textcolor{comment}{* ae\_stream\_writer type is a function pointer for stream  writer  method;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{544 \textcolor{comment}{  this pointer is used by X-\/core for out-\/of-\/core serialization  (say,  to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{545 \textcolor{comment}{  serialize ALGLIB structure directly to managed C\# stream).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{546 \textcolor{comment}{  }}
\DoxyCodeLine{547 \textcolor{comment}{  This function accepts two parameters: pointer to  ANSI  (7-\/bit)  string}}
\DoxyCodeLine{548 \textcolor{comment}{  and pointer-\/sized integer passed to serializer  during  initialization.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{549 \textcolor{comment}{  String being passed is a part of the data stream; aux paramerer may  be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{550 \textcolor{comment}{  arbitrary value intended to be used by actual implementation of  stream}}
\DoxyCodeLine{551 \textcolor{comment}{  writer. String parameter may include spaces and  linefeed  symbols,  it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{552 \textcolor{comment}{  should be written to stream as is.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{553 \textcolor{comment}{  }}
\DoxyCodeLine{554 \textcolor{comment}{  Return value must be zero for success or non-\/zero for failure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{555 \textcolor{comment}{  }}
\DoxyCodeLine{556 \textcolor{comment}{* ae\_stream\_reader type is a function pointer for stream  reader  method;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{557 \textcolor{comment}{  this pointer is used by X-\/core for out-\/of-\/core unserialization (say, to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{558 \textcolor{comment}{  unserialize ALGLIB structure directly from managed C\# stream).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{559 \textcolor{comment}{  }}
\DoxyCodeLine{560 \textcolor{comment}{  This function accepts three parameters: pointer-\/sized integer passed to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{561 \textcolor{comment}{  serializer  during  initialization; number  of  symbols  to  read  from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{562 \textcolor{comment}{  stream; pointer to buffer used to store next  token  read  from  stream}}
\DoxyCodeLine{563 \textcolor{comment}{  (ANSI encoding is used, buffer is large enough to store all symbols and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{564 \textcolor{comment}{  trailing zero symbol).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{565 \textcolor{comment}{  }}
\DoxyCodeLine{566 \textcolor{comment}{  Number of symbols to read is always positive.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{567 \textcolor{comment}{  }}
\DoxyCodeLine{568 \textcolor{comment}{  After being called by X-\/core, this function must:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{569 \textcolor{comment}{  * skip all space and linefeed characters from the current  position  at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{570 \textcolor{comment}{    the stream and until first non-\/space non-\/linefeed character is found}}
\DoxyCodeLine{571 \textcolor{comment}{  * read exactly cnt symbols  from  stream  to  buffer;  check  that  all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{572 \textcolor{comment}{    symbols being read are non-\/space non-\/linefeed ones}}
\DoxyCodeLine{573 \textcolor{comment}{  * append trailing zero symbol to buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{574 \textcolor{comment}{  * return value must be zero on success, non-\/zero if  even  one  of  the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{575 \textcolor{comment}{    conditions above fails. When reader returns non-\/zero value,  contents}}
\DoxyCodeLine{576 \textcolor{comment}{    of buf is not used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{577 \textcolor{comment}{************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{578 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} char(*ae\_stream\_writer)(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *p\_string, ae\_int\_t aux);}
\DoxyCodeLine{579 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} char(*ae\_stream\_reader)(ae\_int\_t aux, ae\_int\_t cnt, \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *p\_buf);}
\DoxyCodeLine{580 }

\DoxyCodeLine{689 }
\DoxyCodeLine{690 \textcolor{comment}{/*************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{691 \textcolor{comment}{Lock.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{692 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{693 \textcolor{comment}{This structure provides OS-\/independent non-\/reentrant lock:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{694 \textcolor{comment}{* under Windows/Posix systems it uses system-\/provided locks}}
\DoxyCodeLine{695 \textcolor{comment}{* under Boost it uses OS-\/independent lock provided by Boost package}}
\DoxyCodeLine{696 \textcolor{comment}{* when no OS is defined, it uses "{}fake lock"{} (just stub which is not thread-\/safe):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{697 \textcolor{comment}{  a) "{}fake lock"{} can be in locked or free mode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{698 \textcolor{comment}{  b) "{}fake lock"{} can be used only from one thread -\/ one which created lock}}
\DoxyCodeLine{699 \textcolor{comment}{  c) when thread acquires free lock, it immediately returns}}
\DoxyCodeLine{700 \textcolor{comment}{  d) when thread acquires busy lock, program is terminated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{701 \textcolor{comment}{     (because lock is already acquired and no one else can free it)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{702 \textcolor{comment}{*************************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{703 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{704 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{705     \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{706 \textcolor{comment}{     * Pointer to \_lock structure. This pointer has type void* in order to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{707 \textcolor{comment}{     * make header file OS-\/independent (lock declaration depends on OS).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{708 \textcolor{comment}{     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{709     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *lock\_ptr;}
\DoxyCodeLine{710     }
\DoxyCodeLine{711     \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{712 \textcolor{comment}{     * For eternal=false this field manages pointer to \_lock structure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{713 \textcolor{comment}{     *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{714 \textcolor{comment}{     * ae\_dyn\_block structure is responsible for automatic deletion of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{715 \textcolor{comment}{     * the memory allocated for the pointer when its frame is destroyed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{716 \textcolor{comment}{     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{717     \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib__impl_1_1ae__dyn__block}{ae\_dyn\_block}} db;}
\DoxyCodeLine{718     }
\DoxyCodeLine{719     \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{720 \textcolor{comment}{     * Whether we have eternal lock object (used by thread pool) or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{721 \textcolor{comment}{     * transient lock. Eternal locks are allocated without using ae\_dyn\_block}}
\DoxyCodeLine{722 \textcolor{comment}{     * structure and do not allow deallocation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{723 \textcolor{comment}{     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{724     ae\_bool eternal;}
\DoxyCodeLine{725 \} \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib__impl_1_1ae__lock}{ae\_lock}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{726 }
\DoxyCodeLine{727 }

\DoxyCodeLine{751 \textcolor{comment}{     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{752     \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib__impl_1_1ae__shared__pool__entry}{ae\_shared\_pool\_entry}}    * \textcolor{keyword}{volatile} recycled\_objects;}
\DoxyCodeLine{753     }
\DoxyCodeLine{754     \textcolor{comment}{/* }}
\DoxyCodeLine{755 \textcolor{comment}{     * list of recycled ENTRIES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{756 \textcolor{comment}{     * 1. this list holds entries which are not used to store recycled objects;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{757 \textcolor{comment}{     *    every time recycled object is retrieved, its entry is moved to this list.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{758 \textcolor{comment}{     * 2. every time object is recycled, we try to fetch entry for him from this list}}
\DoxyCodeLine{759 \textcolor{comment}{     *    before allocating it with malloc()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{760 \textcolor{comment}{     */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{761     \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib__impl_1_1ae__shared__pool__entry}{ae\_shared\_pool\_entry}}    * \textcolor{keyword}{volatile} recycled\_entries;}

\DoxyCodeLine{1132 \textcolor{comment}{* \_force\_malloc\_failure -\/ set this flag to ae\_true in  order  to  enforce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1133 \textcolor{comment}{  failure of ALGLIB malloc(). Useful to debug handling of  errors  during}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1134 \textcolor{comment}{  memory allocation. As long as this flag is set, ALGLIB malloc will fail.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1136 \textcolor{comment}{  malloc failure as soon as \_alloc\_counter\_total increases above value of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1137 \textcolor{comment}{  this variable. This value has no effect if  \_use\_alloc\_counter  is  not}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1371 \textcolor{comment}{Level 1 BLAS functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1372 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1373 \textcolor{comment}{NOTES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1374 \textcolor{comment}{* destination and source should NOT overlap}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1375 \textcolor{comment}{* stride is assumed to be positive, but it is not }}
\DoxyCodeLine{1376 \textcolor{comment}{  assert'ed within function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1377 \textcolor{comment}{* conj\_src parameter specifies whether complex source is conjugated }}
\DoxyCodeLine{1378 \textcolor{comment}{  before processing or not. Pass string which starts with 'N' or 'n'}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1379 \textcolor{comment}{  ("{}No conj"{}, for example) to use unmodified parameter. All other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1380 \textcolor{comment}{  values will result in conjugation of input, but it is recommended}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1381 \textcolor{comment}{  to use "{}Conj"{} in such cases.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1549     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1550     \textcolor{comment}{// This function attaches wrapper object to external x\_vector structure;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1551     \textcolor{comment}{// "{}frozen proxy"{} mode is activated (you can read/write, but can not reallocate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1552     \textcolor{comment}{// and do not own memory of the vector).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1553     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1554     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: initial state of wrapper object is assumed to be initialized;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1555     \textcolor{comment}{//       all previously allocated memory is properly deallocated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1556     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1557     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: x\_vector structure pointed by new\_ptr is used only once; after}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1558     \textcolor{comment}{//       we fetch pointer to memory and its size, this structure is ignored}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1559     \textcolor{comment}{//       and not referenced anymore. So, you can pass pointers to temporary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1560     \textcolor{comment}{//       x-\/structures which are deallocated immediately after you call attach\_to()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1561     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1562     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: state structure is used for error reporting purposes (longjmp on errors).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1563     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1564     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} attach\_to(\mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib__impl_1_1x__vector}{alglib\_impl::x\_vector}} *new\_ptr, \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib__impl_1_1ae__state}{alglib\_impl::ae\_state}} *\_state);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1565 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1566     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1567     \textcolor{comment}{// Assigns RHS to current object. Returns *this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1568     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1569     \textcolor{comment}{// It has several branches depending on target object status:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1570     \textcolor{comment}{// * in case it is proxy object, data are copied into memory pointed by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1571     \textcolor{comment}{//   proxy. Function checks that source has exactly same size as target}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1572     \textcolor{comment}{//   (exception is thrown on failure).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1573     \textcolor{comment}{// * in case it is non-\/proxy object, data allocated by object are cleared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1574     \textcolor{comment}{//   and a copy of RHS is created in target.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1575     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1576     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: this function correctly handles assignments of the object to itself.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1577     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1578     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1ae__vector__wrapper}{ae\_vector\_wrapper}}\& assign(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1ae__vector__wrapper}{ae\_vector\_wrapper}} \&rhs);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1579     }
\DoxyCodeLine{1580     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1581     \textcolor{comment}{// Pointer to ae\_vector structure:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1582     \textcolor{comment}{// * ptr==\&inner\_vec means that wrapper object owns ae\_vector structure and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1583     \textcolor{comment}{//   is responsible for proper deallocation of its memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1584     \textcolor{comment}{// * ptr!=\&inner\_vec means that wrapper object works with someone's other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1585     \textcolor{comment}{//   ae\_vector record and is not responsible for its memory; in this case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1586     \textcolor{comment}{//   inner\_vec is assumed to be uninitialized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1587     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1588     \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib__impl_1_1ae__vector}{alglib\_impl::ae\_vector}} *ptr;}

\DoxyCodeLine{1597     \textcolor{comment}{// Whether this wrapper object is frozen proxy (you may read array, may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1598     \textcolor{comment}{// modify its value, but can not deallocate its memory or resize it) or not.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1599     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1600     \textcolor{comment}{// If is\_frozen\_proxy==true and if:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1601     \textcolor{comment}{// * ptr==\&inner\_vec, it means that wrapper works with its own ae\_vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1602     \textcolor{comment}{//   structure, but this structure points to externally allocated memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1603     \textcolor{comment}{//   This memory is NOT owned by ae\_vector object.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1604     \textcolor{comment}{// * ptr!=\&inner\_vec, it means that wrapper works with externally allocated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1605     \textcolor{comment}{//   and managed ae\_vector structure. Both memory pointed by ae\_vector and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1606     \textcolor{comment}{//   ae\_vector structure itself are not owned by wrapper object.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1607     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1608     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}                   is\_frozen\_proxy;}

\DoxyCodeLine{1807     \textcolor{comment}{// This function attaches wrapper object to external x\_vector structure;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1808     \textcolor{comment}{// "{}frozen proxy"{} mode is activated (you can read/write, but can not reallocate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1809     \textcolor{comment}{// and do not own memory of the vector).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1810     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1811     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: initial state of wrapper object is assumed to be initialized;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1812     \textcolor{comment}{//       all previously allocated memory is properly deallocated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1813     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1814     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: x\_vector structure pointed by new\_ptr is used only once; after}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1815     \textcolor{comment}{//       we fetch pointer to memory and its size, this structure is ignored}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1816     \textcolor{comment}{//       and not referenced anymore. So, you can pass pointers to temporary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1817     \textcolor{comment}{//       x-\/structures which are deallocated immediately after you call attach\_to()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1818     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1819     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: state structure is used for error-\/handling (a longjmp is performed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1820     \textcolor{comment}{//       on allocation error). All previously allocated memory is correctly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1821     \textcolor{comment}{//       freed on error.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1822     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1823     \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} attach\_to(\mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib__impl_1_1x__matrix}{alglib\_impl::x\_matrix}} *new\_ptr, \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib__impl_1_1ae__state}{alglib\_impl::ae\_state}} *\_state);}

\DoxyCodeLine{1832     }
\DoxyCodeLine{1833     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1834     \textcolor{comment}{// Assigns RHS to current object.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1835     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1836     \textcolor{comment}{// It has several branches depending on target object status:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1837     \textcolor{comment}{// * in case it is proxy object, data are copied into memory pointed by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1838     \textcolor{comment}{//   proxy. Function checks that source has exactly same size as target}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1839     \textcolor{comment}{//   (exception is thrown on failure).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1840     \textcolor{comment}{// * in case it is non-\/proxy object, data allocated by object are cleared}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1841     \textcolor{comment}{//   and a copy of RHS is created in target.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1842     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1843     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: this function correctly handles assignments of the object to itself.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1844     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1845     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1ae__matrix__wrapper}{ae\_matrix\_wrapper}} \& assign(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1ae__matrix__wrapper}{ae\_matrix\_wrapper}} \&rhs);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1846     }
\DoxyCodeLine{1847     }
\DoxyCodeLine{1848     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1849     \textcolor{comment}{// Pointer to ae\_matrix structure:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1850     \textcolor{comment}{// * ptr==\&inner\_mat means that wrapper object owns ae\_matrix structure and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1851     \textcolor{comment}{//   is responsible for proper deallocation of its memory}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1852     \textcolor{comment}{// * ptr!=\&inner\_mat means that wrapper object works with someone's other}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1853     \textcolor{comment}{//   ae\_matrix record and is not responsible for its memory; in this case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1854     \textcolor{comment}{//   inner\_mat is assumed to be uninitialized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1855     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1856     \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib__impl_1_1ae__matrix}{alglib\_impl::ae\_matrix}} *ptr;}

\DoxyCodeLine{1858     \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1860     \textcolor{comment}{// Ignored for ptr!=\&inner\_mat.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1861     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1862     \mbox{\hyperlink{structalglib__impl_1_1ae__matrix}{alglib\_impl::ae\_matrix}} inner\_mat;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1863     }
\DoxyCodeLine{1864     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1865     \textcolor{comment}{// Whether this wrapper object is frozen proxy (you may read array, may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1866     \textcolor{comment}{// modify its value, but can not deallocate its memory or resize it) or not.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1867     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1868     \textcolor{comment}{// If is\_frozen\_proxy==true and if:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1869     \textcolor{comment}{// * ptr==\&inner\_vec, it means that wrapper works with its own ae\_vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1870     \textcolor{comment}{//   structure, but this structure points to externally allocated memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1871     \textcolor{comment}{//   This memory is NOT owned by ae\_vector object.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1872     \textcolor{comment}{// * ptr!=\&inner\_vec, it means that wrapper works with externally allocated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1873     \textcolor{comment}{//   and managed ae\_vector structure. Both memory pointed by ae\_vector and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1874     \textcolor{comment}{//   ae\_vector structure itself are not owned by wrapper object.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1875     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1876     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}                   is\_frozen\_proxy;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1877 \};}

\DoxyCodeLine{1962     \textcolor{comment}{// This function attaches array to memory pointed by pContent:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1963     \textcolor{comment}{// * only minor amount of own memory is allocated -\/ O(irows) bytes to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1964     \textcolor{comment}{//   store precomputed pointers; but no costly copying of O(rows*cols)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1965     \textcolor{comment}{//   data is performed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1966     \textcolor{comment}{// * pContent pointer should be valid as long as we work with array}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1967     \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1968     \textcolor{comment}{// After you attach array object to external memory, it becomes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1969     \textcolor{comment}{// "{}frozen"{}: it is possible to read/write array elements, but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1970     \textcolor{comment}{// it is not allowed to resize it (no setlength() calls).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2008 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2009 \textcolor{comment}{/********************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2010 \textcolor{comment}{CSV operations: reading CSV file to real matrix.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2011 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2012 \textcolor{comment}{This function reads CSV  file  and  stores  its  contents  to  double}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2013 \textcolor{comment}{precision 2D array. Format of the data file must conform to RFC  4180}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2014 \textcolor{comment}{specification, with additional notes:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2015 \textcolor{comment}{* file size should be less than 2GB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2016 \textcolor{comment}{* ASCI encoding, UTF-\/8 without BOM (in header names) are supported}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2017 \textcolor{comment}{* any character (comma/tab/space) may be used as field separator,  as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2018 \textcolor{comment}{  long as it is distinct from one used for decimal point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2019 \textcolor{comment}{* multiple subsequent field separators (say, two  spaces) are treated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2020 \textcolor{comment}{  as MULTIPLE separators, not one big separator}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2021 \textcolor{comment}{* both comma and full stop may be used as decimal point. Parser  will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2022 \textcolor{comment}{  automatically determine specific character being used.  Both  fixed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2023 \textcolor{comment}{  and exponential number formats are  allowed.   Thousand  separators}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2024 \textcolor{comment}{  are NOT allowed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2025 \textcolor{comment}{* line may end with \(\backslash\)n (Unix style) or \(\backslash\)r\(\backslash\)n (Windows  style),  parser}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2026 \textcolor{comment}{  will automatically adapt to chosen convention}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2027 \textcolor{comment}{* escaped fields (ones in double quotes) are not supported}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2028 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2029 \textcolor{comment}{INPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2030 \textcolor{comment}{    filename        relative/absolute path}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2031 \textcolor{comment}{    separator       character used to separate fields.  May  be  ' ',}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2032 \textcolor{comment}{                    ',', '\(\backslash\)t'. Other separators are possible too.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2033 \textcolor{comment}{    flags           several values combined with bitwise OR:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2034 \textcolor{comment}{                    * alglib::CSV\_SKIP\_HEADERS -\/  if present, first row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2035 \textcolor{comment}{                      contains headers  and  will  be  skipped.   Its}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2036 \textcolor{comment}{                      contents is used to determine fields count, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2037 \textcolor{comment}{                      that's all.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2038 \textcolor{comment}{                    If no flags are specified, default value 0x0  (or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2039 \textcolor{comment}{                    alglib::CSV\_DEFAULT, which is same) should be used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2040 \textcolor{comment}{                    }}
\DoxyCodeLine{2041 \textcolor{comment}{OUTPUT PARAMETERS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2042 \textcolor{comment}{    out             2D matrix, CSV file parsed with atof()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2043 \textcolor{comment}{    }}
\DoxyCodeLine{2044 \textcolor{comment}{HANDLING OF SPECIAL CASES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2045 \textcolor{comment}{* file does not exist -\/ alglib::ap\_error exception is thrown}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2046 \textcolor{comment}{* empty file -\/ empty array is returned (no exception)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2047 \textcolor{comment}{* skip\_first\_row=true, only one row in file -\/ empty array is returned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2048 \textcolor{comment}{* field contents is not recognized by atof() -\/ field value is replaced}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2049 \textcolor{comment}{  by 0.0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2050 \textcolor{comment}{********************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2051 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if !defined(AE\_NO\_EXCEPTIONS)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2052 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} read\_csv(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *filename, \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} separator, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} flags, \mbox{\hyperlink{classalglib_1_1real__2d__array}{alglib::real\_2d\_array}} \&out);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2053 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2054 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2055 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2056 \textcolor{comment}{/********************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2057 \textcolor{comment}{This function activates trace output, with trace log being  saved  to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2058 \textcolor{comment}{file (appended to the end).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2059 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2060 \textcolor{comment}{Tracing allows us to study behavior of ALGLIB solvers  and  to  debug}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2061 \textcolor{comment}{their failures:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2062 \textcolor{comment}{* tracing is  limited  by one/several ALGLIB parts specified by means}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2063 \textcolor{comment}{  of trace tags, like "{}SLP"{} (for SLP solver) or "{}OPTGUARD"{}  (OptGuard}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2064 \textcolor{comment}{  integrity checker).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2065 \textcolor{comment}{* some ALGLIB solvers support hierarchies of trace tags which activate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2066 \textcolor{comment}{  different kinds of tracing. Say, "{}SLP"{} defines some basic  tracing,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2067 \textcolor{comment}{  but "{}SLP.PROBING"{} defines more detailed and costly tracing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2068 \textcolor{comment}{* generally, "{}TRACETAG.SUBTAG"{}   also  implicitly  activates  logging}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2069 \textcolor{comment}{  which is activated by "{}TRACETAG"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2070 \textcolor{comment}{* you may define multiple trace tags by separating them with  commas,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2071 \textcolor{comment}{  like "{}SLP,OPTGUARD,SLP.PROBING"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2072 \textcolor{comment}{* trace tags are case-\/insensitive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2073 \textcolor{comment}{* spaces/tabs are NOT allowed in the tags string}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2074 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2075 \textcolor{comment}{Trace log is saved to file "{}filename"{}, which is opened in the  append}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2076 \textcolor{comment}{mode. If no file with such name  can  be  opened,  tracing  won't  be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2077 \textcolor{comment}{performed (but no exception will be generated).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2078 \textcolor{comment}{********************************************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2079 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} trace\_file(std::string tags, std::string filename);}
\DoxyCodeLine{2080 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2081 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2082 \textcolor{comment}{/********************************************************************}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2084 \textcolor{comment}{********************************************************************/}}
